&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;On December 31, 2014, the Company&#13;entered into a Securities Purchase Agreement (&amp;#147;2014 Agreement&amp;#148;) with certain accredited investors to sell to the Purchasers&#13;an aggregate of up to $500,000 of principal amount of notes due December 31, 2015 representing the Purchasers&amp;#146; subscription&#13;amount. The 2014 Agreement defines certain covenants and provides for a purchase price reset for a period of three years, unless&#13;the securities have been assigned, whereby should the Company issue or sell any shares of common stock or any common stock equivalents&#13;at a price less than the Purchasers&amp;#146; conversion price per share, the Company will be required to issue additional shares&#13;of common stock to the Purchasers for no additional consideration resulting in a share dilution adjustment, as defined. The 2014&#13;Agreement also provides a Most Favored Nations Provision whereby if the Company issues or sells any common stock at terms more&#13;favorable within three years, then the Company will be required to amend the 2014 Agreement to provide such favorable terms to&#13;the Purchasers. The Company paid $33,000 in legal and escrow agent fees, a placement agency fee of $20,000 in the form of a note&#13;payable, substantially similar to the Purchasers&amp;#146; notes and issued 64,000, shares of its common stock valued at $640,000&#13;and $20,000 as due diligence fees, all of which have been recorded as debt issuance costs on the accompanying consolidated financial&#13;statements and is being charged to operations over the twelve months ended December 31, 2015. The Company recorded amortization&#13;expense of $713,000 and $0 on the debt issuance costs during the year ended December 31, 2015 and 2014, respectively. At December&#13;31, 2015 the maturity date of the notes were extended to December 31, 2016.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Under the 2014 Agreement, the Company sold an aggregate&#13;of $425,000 in Secured Convertible Notes (&amp;#147;Notes&amp;#148;) and issued an additional $20,000 Note for placement fees.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;The&#13;Company fulfilled its obligations as defined by certain equity requirements; therefore, the Notes will be convertible into shares&#13;of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock.&amp;#160; Under certain conditions defined in the agreement, the Company has the option to convert&#13;the Notes into shares of the Company's common stock.&amp;#160; Since the equity obligations were met during 2015 the Notes accrued&#13;interest at 10% per annum through June 30, 2015.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;The original conversion price on the Note was $6.00, and has subsequently&#13;reduced to $0.30 at December 31, 2015.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Each Holder of the Notes has been&#13;granted a security interest in assets of the Company in accordance with a Security Agreement. The Security Agreement provides the&#13;Collateral Agent a security interest in all goods, machinery, equipment, contract rights and intangibles in the event of a default&#13;under the Agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;In connection with this 2014 Agreement,&#13;and under the anti-dilution provisions of the February 2014 private placement, on December 31, 2014, the Company issued an aggregate&#13;of 160,093 shares of common stock and 13,333 warrants to purchase common shares at $6.00 per share to existing stockholders holding&#13;securities purchased in that offering. This reflects the post-split adjustment to shares issued and price per share. The fair value&#13;of the 13,333 warrants issued in 2014 were valued at $122,807 using the Black-Scholes Pricing model and was reflected as a change&#13;in the derivative liability in the 2014 statement of operations.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;In addition, the pricing of this&#13;2014 Agreement triggered the pricing reset provision in the 3,333 warrants issued in the February 14, 2014 private placement. Such&#13;triggering resulted in the exercise price of the previously issued warrants resetting to $6.00 from $30.00 at December 31, 2014.&#13;The exercise price was further reduced to $0.30 as a result of additional financing in 2015. At December 31, 2015, using the Black-Scholes&#13;Pricing Model, the Company re-valued the remaining February 2014 warrants at $1,591 a decrease in fair value of $28,208 from December&#13;31, 2014 ($29,799) and a decrease in fair value of $569,409 since inception. The decrease in this derivative liability during 2014&#13;amounted to $541,201.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;At December 31, 2015, the 13,333&#13;ratchet warrants granted at December 31, 2014 were re-valued using the Black-Scholes Pricing Model at $6,633, a decrease in fair&#13;value of $116,174 from December 31, 2014 ($122,807).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The significant assumptions utilized&#13;by the Company in the valuation of these warrants at December 31, 2015 and 2014 were as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;Risk Free Rate of Return:&amp;#9;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;1.31%&amp;#9;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;0.25%&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;On September 21, 2015, the Company&#13;entered into a Securities Purchase Agreement (&amp;#147;Sept 2015 Agreement&amp;#148;) with certain accredited investors to sell to the&#13;Purchasers an aggregate of up to $250,000 of principal amount of notes due September 30, 2016, representing the Purchasers&amp;#146;&#13;subscription amount. The new offering is substantially the same terms and conditions as the December 2014 Notes. In connection&#13;with the new offering, the Company issued allonges to the December 2014 Notes increasing the principal amount of the Notes (&amp;#34;Allonges&amp;#34;)&#13;pursuant to the terms of the new offering with such Allonges having a maturity date of September 30, 2016 and a conversion price&#13;equal to $1.00 per share (subject to further reduction), at September 21, 2015. The conversion price was reduced to $0.30 at December&#13;31, 2015 as a result of a subsequent financing.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;The Sept 2015 Agreement defines&#13;certain covenants and provides for a purchase price reset for a period of three years, unless the securities have been assigned,&#13;whereby should the Company issue or sell any shares of common stock or any common stock equivalents at a price less than the Purchasers&amp;#146;&#13;conversion price per share, the Company will be required to issue additional shares of common stock to the Purchasers for no additional&#13;consideration resulting in a share dilution adjustment, as defined. The Sept 2015 Agreement also provides a Most Favored Nations&#13;Provision whereby if the Company issues or sells any common stock at terms more favorable&lt;b&gt; &lt;/b&gt;within three years, then the&#13;Company will be required to amend the Sept 2015 Agreement to provide such favorable terms to the Purchasers. The Company paid&#13;$12,500 in legal fees, a placement agency fee of $25,000 in the form of a note payable, substantially similar to the Purchasers&amp;#146;&#13;notes, all of which was recorded as debt issuance costs on the accompanying consolidated financial statements and will be charged&#13;to operations over the twelve months ended September 30, 2016 or to the date of conversion, if earlier.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Under the Sept 2015 Agreement,&#13;the Company sold an aggregate of $250,000 in Secured Convertible Notes and issued an additional $25,000 Note for placement fees.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;Once&#13;the Company has fulfilled its obligations as defined by certain equity requirements, the Notes will be convertible into shares&#13;of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock.&amp;#160; Under certain conditions defined in the agreement, the Company has the option to convert&#13;the Notes into shares of the Company's common stock.&amp;#160; Until the equity obligations are met, the Notes bear interest at 10%,&#13;per annum.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;Interest will be earned at a rate of 10% for the twelve months ending September 30, 2016 or to the date&#13;of conversion, whichever is earlier. The conversion price for the Note and accrued interest was equal to $1.00 per share at September&#13;21, 2015 subject to adjustments as stock dividends and stock splits, as defined. At December 31, 2015, the conversion price was&#13;reduced to $0.30.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Each Holder of the Notes has been&#13;granted a security interest in assets of the Company in accordance with a Security Agreement. The Security Agreement provides&#13;the Collateral Agent a security interest in all goods, machinery, equipment, contract rights and intangibles in the event of a&#13;default under the Agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;On December 31, 2015, the Company&#13;entered into a Securities Purchase Agreement (&amp;#147;Dec 2015 Agreement&amp;#148;) with certain accredited investors to sell to the&#13;Purchasers an aggregate of up to $500,000 of principal amount of notes due December 31 2016, representing the Purchasers&amp;#146;&#13;subscription amount. The new offering is substantially the same terms and conditions as the December 2014 Notes.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;The Dec 2015 Agreement defines certain covenants and provides for a purchase price reset for a period of three&#13;years, unless the securities have been assigned, whereby should the Company issue or sell any shares of common stock or any common&#13;stock equivalents at a price less than the Purchasers&amp;#146; conversion price per share, the Company will be required to issue&#13;additional shares of common stock to the Purchasers for no additional consideration resulting in a share dilution adjustment,&#13;as defined. The Dec 2015 Agreement also provides a Most Favored Nations Provision whereby if the Company issues or sells any common&#13;stock at terms more favorable within three years, then the Company will be required to amend the Dec 2015 Agreement to provide&#13;such favorable terms to the Purchasers. The Company paid $18,000 in legal fees and a placement agency fee of $50,000 in the form&#13;of a note payable, with substantially similar to the Purchasers&amp;#146; notes, all of which was recorded as debt issuance costs&#13;on the accompanying consolidated financial statements and will be charged to operations over the twelve months ended December&#13;31, 2016 or to the date of conversion, if earlier.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Under the Dec 2015 Agreement,&#13;the Company sold an aggregate of $500,000 in Secured Convertible Notes (&amp;#147;Notes&amp;#148;) and issued an additional $50,000&#13;Note for placement fees.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;Once the Company has fulfilled its obligations as defined by certain equity requirements,&#13;the Notes will be convertible into shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock.&amp;#160; Under certain conditions defined in the agreement,&#13;the Company has the option to convert the Notes into shares of the Company's common stock.&amp;#160; Until the equity obligations&#13;are met, the Notes bear interest at 10%, per annum.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;Interest will be earned at a rate of 10% for the twelve months&#13;ending December 31, 2016 or to the date of conversion, whichever is earlier. The conversion price for the Note and accrued interest&#13;is equal to $0.30 per share, subject to adjustments as stock dividends and stock splits, as defined.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Each Holder of the Notes has&#13;been granted a security interest in assets of the Company in accordance with a Security Agreement. The Security Agreement provides&#13;the Collateral Agent a security interest in all goods, machinery, equipment, contract rights and intangibles in the event of a&#13;default under the Agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;In connection with the Sept 2015 and Dec. 2015 Agreements, and under&#13;the anti-dilution provisions of the December 2014 private placement,&amp;#160;the Company is required to issue an aggregate of 2,611,003&#13;shares of common stock&amp;#160;&amp;#160;to existing stockholders holding securities purchased in that offering,&amp;#160;&amp;#160;of which 1,249,569&#13;were issued as of December 31, 2015.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white&gt;The Company has&#13;determined that the convertible notes issued on December 31, 2014, September 21, 2015 and December 31, 2015 contain provisions&#13;that protect holders from future issuances of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock at prices below such convertible notes&amp;#146; respective&#13;conversion price and these provisions result in modification of the conversion price to issue additional common shares based on&#13;a variable that is not an input to the fair value of a &amp;#147;fixed-for-fixed&amp;#148; option as defined under FASB ASC Topic No.&#13;815 &amp;#150; 40 and the conversion feature represents an embedded derivative that requires bifurcation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.25in; background-color: white&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white&gt;The fair values&#13;of the Convertible Notes Offering were recognized as derivative instruments at issuance and are measured at fair value at each&#13;reporting period. The embedded derivative on the 2014 Agreement was valued at $594,963 using a binomial valuation model at December&#13;31, 2014. In addition during 2015 the Company recognized derivative liabilities aggregating $1,439,432 in connection with the Sept&#13;2015 and Dec 2015 fund raising. At December 31, 2015, the embedded conversion derivative for all three debt financings was revalued&#13;to $2,224,362 and the Company recorded an increase in the derivative liability related to its convertible debt of $189,967. The&#13;assumptions considered in the valuation model for the December 31, 2014 notes at December 31, 2015 and 2014 were:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Change in fair value&amp;#9;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;( 35,676)&amp;#9;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Balance, December 31, 2015&amp;#9;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;u&gt;$2,232,586&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;The derivative liability&#13;at December 31, 2015 consists of debt conversions of $2,224,362 ($594,963 - 2014) and warrants of $8,224 ($233,867 - 2014).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;b&gt;Accounting for Convertible&#13;Debt&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Under the initial accounting for&#13;the December 2014 Offering the Company allocated the proceeds to the embedded conversion derivative liability, which exceeded&#13;the $445,000 face amount of the convertible debt at the issuance date. The proceeds allocated to the embedded conversion derivative&#13;liability were recognized as a discount to the convertible debt. As of December 31, 2014, the Company recorded aggregate debt discounts&#13;of $445,000 related to the conversion rights and recorded $149,963 of expense related to the excess value of the derivative over&#13;the face amount of the convertible debt.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;Under&#13;the September 21, 2015 &lt;/font&gt;offering &lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;the Company allocated the proceeds to the embedded conversion&#13;derivative liability, which exceeded the $275,000&lt;/font&gt; face amount of the &lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;additional convertible&#13;debt at the issuance date. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;Under&#13;the December 31, 2015 &lt;/font&gt;offering &lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;the Company allocated the proceeds to the embedded conversion&#13;derivative liability, which exceeded the $550,000&lt;/font&gt; face amount of the &lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;additional convertible&#13;debt at the issuance date. &amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;As a result, upon issuance of the&#13;two 2015 debt offerings, the Company recorded a debt discount of $825,000 and recorded a loss of $614,432 related to the excess&#13;value of the $1,439,432 the derivative over the $825,000 face amount of the convertible debt.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;The debt discount is accreted to&#13;interest expense over the life of the convertible debentures using an effective interest method. For the year ended December 31,&#13;2015, the Company amortized $609,288 of the debt discount. In addition, amortization of deferred debt issuance costs amounted to&#13;$722,375 for the year ended December 31,2015.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;2014&#13;Financing&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;On&#13;February 14, 2014, the Company sold to certain accredited investors pursuant to a Subscription Agreement, an aggregate of 33,333&#13;shares of its common stock, 26,667 shares of the Series C Preferred Stock and five year warrants to purchase up to an aggregate&#13;of 59,999 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock at an exercise price of $30, per share, for gross proceeds of $1,800,000.&#13;Until the earlier of (i) three years from the closing of the Offering or (ii) such time as no investor holds any shares of common&#13;stock underlying warrants or underlying the Series C Preferred Stock, in the event the Company issues or sells common stock at&#13;a per share price equal to less than $30.00 per share, as adjusted, the Company has agreed to issue additional securities such&#13;that the aggregate purchase price paid by the investor shall equal the lower price issuance, subject to certain exceptions, as&#13;defined. The Company recorded a derivative liability related to the reset feature on the exercise price of the warrants to purchase&#13;common stock issued by the Company.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;connection with the Offering, the Company granted the investors &amp;#147;piggy-back&amp;#148; registration rights and the investors are&#13;entitled to a right of participation in future financings conducted by the Company for a period of twenty-four months.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;2014 the Company paid placement agent fees of $144,000 in cash, issued an aggregate of 600 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common&#13;stock and issued a five year warrant to purchase up to 5,399 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock at a price of $30 per share,&#13;as commission in connection with the sale of the shares and warrants. In addition, the Company permitted the conversion of an&#13;aggregate of $13,500 of unpaid fees owed to a consultant into 450 shares and warrants at the Offering price. In conjunction with&#13;the Offering, $100,000 was placed in an escrow account to be used for auditing and legal fees. As of December 31, 2015, the balance&#13;of the escrow account was $0 and $12,500 in 2014.&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;On&#13;February 14, 2014, as a component of the Subscription Agreement, the Company issued an aggregate of 66,333 warrants with a fair&#13;value of $11,361,278 determined using the Black-Scholes Pricing Model.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Pursuant&#13;to the subscription agreement in 2014, certain members of the Company&amp;#146;s management agreed to invest an aggregate of $250,000&#13;in exchange for 8,333 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock within 30 days of the closing, on the same terms of the agreement.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Series&#13;B Convertible Preferred Stock&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;In&#13;April 2013, the Company&amp;#146;s Board of Directors authorized four (4) shares of preferred stock, par value $0.0001 per share as&#13;Series B Convertible Preferred Stock (the &amp;#147;Series B Preferred Stock&amp;#148;) and issued one share of Series B Preferred Stock&#13;to each of the Company&amp;#146;s three senior members of management. Each share of Series B Preferred Stock is entitled such number&#13;of votes on all matters submitted to stockholders that is equal to (i) the product of (a) the number of shares of Series B Preferred&#13;Stock held by such holder, (b) the number of issued and outstanding shares of the Company&amp;#146;s Common Stock (taking into account&#13;the effective outstanding voting rights of the Series B Preferred Stock), as of the record date for the vote and (c) 0.13334 less&#13;(ii) the number of shares of Common Stock beneficially held by such holder on such date. Additionally, on the six month anniversary&#13;date of issuance of the Series B Preferred Stock, each outstanding share of Series B Preferred Stock was to automatically, and&#13;without further action on the part of the holder, convert into such number of fully paid and non-assessable shares of Common Stock&#13;as would cause the holder to own, along with any other securities of the Company&amp;#146;s beneficially owned on the conversion date&#13;by them 13.334% of the issued and outstanding Common Stock, calculated on the conversion date. On October 25, 2013, the Company&#13;amended and restated the Certificate of Designation for Series B Convertible Preferred Stock to extend the date on which the Series&#13;B Shares would automatically convert into such number of fully paid and non-assessable shares of common stock, from the date six&#13;months from the date of issuance (October 26, 2013) to the twelfth month anniversary of the date of issuance of the shares of&#13;Series B Preferred Stock (April 26, 2014) which on April 22, 2014, was further extended to an indefinite date. The Company previously&#13;recorded the three shares of Series B Convertible Preferred Stock as stock-based compensation using the then current estimate&#13;of the number of shares that would convert to shares of common stock of the Company based on the shares outstanding and current&#13;price per share at each balance sheet date. As of December 31, 2014, the Company recalculated the estimated shares issuable to&#13;be 216,670 and recorded stock-based compensation of $2,166,707 for the year then ended. The estimate is based on the current common&#13;shares outstanding at December 31, 2014, a stock price of $10.00 per share, and is subject to adjustment based on any additional&#13;common shares issued.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;On&#13;March 2, 2015, the Series B Convertible Preferred Stock which was then outstanding was cancelled and as a result, the Company&amp;#146;s&#13;obligation to issue any common shares in connection therewith ended. The Company has accounted for the cancellation of the Series&#13;B and issuance of the Series D Preferred Stock as an extinguishment. Accordingly, for the year ended December 31, 2015, the Company&#13;recorded an aggregate gain of $3,420,804 within stockholders&amp;#146; deficit equal to the difference between the $667,664 fair value&#13;of the Series D preferred stock and the $4,088,468 carrying amount of the Series B preferred stock extinguished. The gain on extinguishment&#13;is reflected in the calculation of net income attributable to common stockholders in 2015.&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;Series&#13;C Convertible Preferred Stock&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;On&#13;February 12, 2014, the Company designated and authorized to issue 26,667 shares of Series C Convertible Preferred Stock (&amp;#147;Series&#13;C Preferred Stock&amp;#148;), par value $0.0001, per share. Each holder of Series C Preferred Stock shall be entitled to vote all&#13;matters submitted to shareholder vote and shall be entitled to the number of votes for each shares of Series C owned at the designated&#13;record date. Each holder of Series C Preferred Stock may convert any or all of such shares into fully paid and non-assessable&#13;shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock in an amount equal to one share of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock for each one shares&#13;of Series C Preferred Stock.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;On&#13;September 21, 2015, in connection with the terms of a ratchet provision for certain warrants issued in 2014, the Company revised&#13;the conversion right so that holders of Series C Preferred Stock may, from time to time, convert any or all of such holder's shares&#13;of Series C Preferred Stock into fully paid and non-assessable shares of common stock in an amount equal 100 shares of the Company's&#13;common stock (the &amp;#34;Common Stock&amp;#34;) for each one (1) share of Series C Preferred stock surrendered.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif&gt;As&#13;a result of this modification, the Company recorded a deemed dividend on Series C Preferred Stock in the amount&#13;of $1,089,000.&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font: 11pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;Series&#13;D Convertible Preferred Stock&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif&gt;On,&#13;March 2, 2015, the Board of Directors of the Company designated and authorized to issue 3,000 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s authorized&#13;Preferred Stock, par value $0.0001 per share, as Series D Convertible Preferred Stock. Each holder of the Series D Preferred Stock&#13;(&amp;#147;Series D&amp;#148;) shall have the number of votes on all matters submitted to the stockholders that is equal to the greater&#13;of one hundred votes for each one share of Series D and such number of votes per share of Series D that when added to the votes&#13;per shares of all other shares of Series D shall equal 50.1% of the outstanding voting record. The Series D are convertible into&#13;common stock in an amount equal to one share of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock for each one share of Series D. On March 9, 2015,&#13;the Company issued 1,000 shares of the Series D to each of three officers of the Company.&amp;#9;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;On&#13;February 4, 2014, the holders representing a majority of the then outstanding shares of capital stock of the Company voted and&#13;approved and permitted the Company to increase the number of authorized shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock from 400,000,000&#13;to 525,000,000. On March 12, 2015, the holders representing a majority of the then outstanding shares of capital stock of the&#13;Company voted and approved and permitted the Company to increase the number of authorized shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common&#13;stock from 525,000,000 to 750,000,000.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif&gt;As&#13;discussed in Note 8, the warrants issued related to these capital raises were deemed to be derivative liabilities and required&#13;additional measurement at fair value. Accordingly, the proceeds from these equity financings were first allocated to such fair&#13;value instruments (the warrants), with the residual proceeds, if any, being allocated to the instruments not subsequently marked&#13;to fair value.&amp;#160;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;As of December 31, 2015, management&#13;has evaluated and concluded that there are no significant uncertain tax positions requiring recognition in the Company's financial&#13;statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;As of December 31, 2015 and 2014,&#13;the Company has net operating loss carryforwards of approximately $7,810,000 and $5,600,000, respectively, to reduce future Federal&#13;and state taxable income through 2033 and $4,800,000 and $4,100,000, respectively of temporary differences in the timing of the&#13;deduction for certain stock-based compensation. However, as a result of the recent and potential changes in the share ownership&#13;of the Company, future utilization of the net operating losses may be limited pursuant to Section 382 of the Internal Revenue Service.&#13;The maximum net operating loss carryforward which could be utilized pursuant to Section 382 for Be Active Brands is $185,000 a&#13;year, based on the approximately $2,500,000 losses incurred prior to the 2013 Merger.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Since at present realization of&#13;the Company&amp;#146;s related deferred tax assets of $4,800,000 at December 31, 2015 and $3,688,000 at December 31, 2014 is not considered&#13;more likely than not, a valuation allowance of $4,800,000 at December 30, 2015 and $3,688,000 at December 31, 2014 have been provided.&#13;The valuation allowance increased by $1,112,000 from December 31, 2014. Certain charges for operations for the years ended December&#13;31, 2015 and 2014 related to derivative liabilities resulting from equity and debt issuances have no income tax effect and are&#13;not considered above.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

   &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;Net sales&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 11.5pt&gt;(128,995)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; padding-right: 5.4pt; padding-left: 5.4pt;  Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;An officer and Director of the&#13;Company was a partner of a public accounting firm providing non-audit accounting services to the Company through October 30, 2014.&#13;Subsequent to October 2014, all non-audit accounting services were performed by the officer/director of the Company in conjunction&#13;with an independent consultant. For the years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014, the Company incurred fees of $0 and $66,666, respectively,&#13;to the accounting firm for accounting and tax services.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Effective January 9, 2013, the&#13;Company adopted a Stock Option Plan (&amp;#147;Plan&amp;#148;) to provide an incentive to attract, retain and reward persons performing&#13;services, including employees, consultants, directors and other persons determined by the Board, through equity awards. The Plan&#13;shall continue in effect until its termination by the Board provided that all awards are granted within ten years, as defined.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On January 6, 2016 an advance payable to&#13;an officer at December 31, 2015, in the amount of $111,000 was repaid.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On January 8, 2016 the company issued an&#13;additional 668,433 of common shares due to existing shareholders based on various ratchet provisions of prior capital raises.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On January 13, 2016, the Company issued an&#13;aggregate of 150,000 shares of common stock at $0.30 per share to an existing stockholder who converted a part of his note payable&#13;in the amount of $45,000.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The consolidated financial statements&#13;include the accounts of the Company and its wholly-owned subsidiary and have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles&#13;generally accepted in the United States of America. All significant intercompany transactions and balances have been eliminated.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company considers the carrying&#13;amounts of financial instruments, including cash, accounts receivable, accounts payable, and accrued expenses to approximate their&#13;fair values because of their relatively short maturities. The fair value of convertible notes payable approximate their face value.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Fair value is defined as the exchange&#13;price that would be received for an asset or paid to transfer a liability (an exit price) in the principal or most advantageous&#13;market for the asset or liability in an orderly transaction between market participants on the measurement date. Valuation techniques&#13;used to measure fair value must maximize the use of observable inputs and minimize the use of unobservable inputs. The Company&#13;uses a fair value hierarchy based on three levels of inputs, of which the first two are considered observable and the last unobservable,&#13;that may be used to measure fair value which are the following:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Level 1 &amp;#150; Unadjusted quoted&#13;prices in active markets that are accessible at measurement date for identical assets or liabilities.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Level 2 - Inputs other than Level&#13;1 that are observable, either directly or indirectly, such as quoted prices for similar assets or liabilities; quoted prices in&#13;markets that are not active; or other inputs that are observable or can be corroborated by observable market data for substantially&#13;the full term of the assets or liabilities.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Level 3 - Unobservable inputs that&#13;are supported by little or no market activity and that are significant to the fair value of the assets or liabilities and less&#13;observable from objective sources.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;Property and equipment are recorded&#13;at cost and depreciated over their estimated useful lives using the straight-line method.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company provides for income&#13;taxes under FASB ASC 740 &amp;#150; &lt;i&gt;Income Taxes&lt;/i&gt;, which requires the use of an assets and liabilities approach in accounting&#13;for income taxes. Deferred tax assets and liabilities are recorded based on the differences between the financial statement and&#13;tax bases of assets and liabilities and the tax rates in effect when these differences are expected to reverse. A valuation allowance&#13;is provided when realization of deferred tax assets is not considered more likely than not.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company&amp;#146;s policy is to&#13;classify income tax assessments, if any, for interest in interest expense and for penalties in general and administrative expenses.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;As of December 31, 2015, management&#13;has evaluated and concluded that there are no significant uncertain tax positions requiring recognition in the Company's consolidated&#13;financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;In February 2016, a pronouncement was issued that creates new&#13;accounting and reporting guidelines for leasing arrangements. The new guidance requires organizations that lease assets to recognize&#13;assets and liabilities on the balance sheet related to the rights and obligations created by those leases, regardless of whether&#13;they are classified as finance or operating leases. The new standard is effective for annual reporting periods beginning after&#13;December 15, 2018, including interim periods within that reporting period, with early application permitted. The new standard is&#13;to be applied using a modified retrospective approach. The Company is in the process of evaluating the impact of the new pronouncement&#13;on its consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 12pt/12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;In April 2015, the FASB issued ASU No. 2015-03, &amp;#34;Simplifying&#13;the Presentation of Debt Issuance Costs&amp;#148;. ASU 2015-03 requires that debt issuance costs related to a recognized debt liability&#13;be presented in the balance sheet as a direct deduction from the carrying amount of that debt liability, consistent with debt discounts.&#13;The standard is effective for annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2015, and interim periods within those years,&#13;with early adoption permitted. The Company is currently evaluating the potential impact this standard may have on the consolidated&#13;financial statements and the timing of adoption.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;In May 2014, the Financial Accounting Standards Board (&amp;#34;FASB&amp;#34;)&#13;issued accounting guidance, &amp;#34;Revenue from Contracts with Customers.&amp;#34; The core principle of the new standard is for companies&#13;to recognize revenue to depict the transfer of goods or services to customers in amounts that reflect the consideration (that is,&#13;payment) to which the company expects to be entitled in exchange for those goods or services.The standard will be effective for&#13;fiscal years and interim periods within those years beginning after December 15, 2017. Accordingly, the Company will adopt this&#13;standard in the first quarter of fiscal year 2018. The Company is currently evaluating the impact this guidance will have on the&#13;consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27.35pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;In August 2014, the FASB issued ASU 2014-15, &amp;#34;Presentation&#13;of Financial Statements-Going Concern&amp;#34;. This ASU is intended to define management's responsibility to evaluate whether there&#13;is substantial doubt about an organization's ability to continue as a going concern and to provide related footnote disclosures.&#13;It is effective for annual periods beginning after December 15, 2016, with early adoption permitted. The Company does not expect&#13;it to have a material effect on the Company's consolidated financial condition, results of operations, and cash flows.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;At December 31, 2015, the 13,333&#13;ratchet warrants granted at December 31, 2014 were re-valued using the Black-Scholes Pricing Model at $6,633, a decrease in fair&#13;value of $116,174 from December 31, 2014 ($122,807).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The significant assumptions utilized&#13;by the Company in the valuation of these warrants at December 31, 2015 and 2014 were as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#9;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;u&gt;2015&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#9;&lt;u&gt;2014&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 9.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;Market Price: &amp;#9;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;$0.55&amp;#9;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;$10.00&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 11.5pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;Basic income (loss) per share is computed by dividing the net income&#13;or loss attributable to the common stockholders by the weighted average number of shares of common stock outstanding during the&#13;period. Fully diluted income (loss) per share is computed similar to basic income (loss) per share except that the denominator&#13;for fully diluted income per share is increased to include the number of additional common shares that would have been outstanding&#13;if the potential common shares had been issued in order to present their dilutive effect unless the effect of such potential shares&#13;would be antidilutive. Potential common shares consist of incremental common shares issuable upon the exercise of warrants, convertible&#13;preferred shares and convertible notes payable. In addition, in computing net income (loss) per share on a fully diluted basis,&#13;the Company adjusts for the interest expense on convertible debt as if the debt had been converted for all periods presented.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Employment Agreements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;Effective January 9, 2013, extended and revised October 1, 2014,&#13;the Company entered into an employment agreement with its chief financial officer for a term of three years, to be automatically&#13;renewed for successive one year periods thereafter unless either party provides written notice of intention not to renew the agreement.&#13;The agreement provides for a base annual salary of $135,000, paid in periodic installments in accordance with the Company&amp;#146;s&#13;regular payroll practices and includes other Company benefits.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;The Agreement entitles the officer to future grants under&#13;the Company&amp;#146;s 2013 Equity Incentive Plan.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;In addition, the Company has awarded the Officer a bonus of 6,385 shares&#13;of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock at December 31, 2014 which vested immediately and were purchased by the Officer at par value.&#13;These shares were issued on January 9, 2015. Total compensation for these shares recorded at December 31, 2014 was $63,216 based&#13;on the traded price of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock on that date.&amp;#160; There were no bonuses awarded the officer in 2015.&amp;#160;&#13;Costs incurred pursuant to this agreement for the year ended December 31, 2015 and 2014 were $145,000 and $96,793 respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;Effective January 9, 2013, extended and revised October 1, 2014,&#13;the Company entered into an employment agreement with its former President for a term of three years, to be automatically renewed&#13;for successive one year periods thereafter unless either party provides written notice of intention not to renew the agreement.&#13;The agreement provides for a base annual salary of $150,000, paid in periodic installments in accordance with the Company&amp;#146;s&#13;regular payroll practices and an annual bonus, subject to claw-back provisions, based on reaching certain financial targets as&#13;defined and includes other Company benefits. The Agreement entitles the officer to future grants under the Company&amp;#146;s 2013&#13;Equity Incentive Plan.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;In addition, the Company had awarded the Officer a bonus of 5,000 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s&#13;common stock at December 31, 2014 which vested immediately and were purchased by the Officer at par value. These shares were issued&#13;on January 9, 2015.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;Total compensation for these shares recorded at December 31, 2014 was $49,500 based on the traded&#13;price of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock on that date.&amp;#160; There were no bonuses awarded the officer in 2015.&amp;#160; Costs incurred&#13;pursuant to the Officer&amp;#146;s employment agreements for years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014 was $126,154 and $151,731, respectively.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;On&#13;June 19, 2015, the Company re-appointed the former President as a member of the Board of Directors and Vice-President.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;Effective January 9, 2013, extended and revised October 1, 2014,&#13;the Company entered into an employment agreement with its secretary and current Interim President for a term of three years, to&#13;be automatically renewed for successive one year periods thereafter unless either party provides written notice of intention not&#13;to renew the agreement. The agreement provides for a base annual&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;salary of $135,000, paid in periodic installments&#13;in accordance with the Company&amp;#146;s regular payroll practices and an annual bonus, subject to claw-back provisions, based on&#13;reaching certain financial targets as defined and include other Company benefits. The Agreement entitles the officer to future&#13;grants under the Company&amp;#146;s 2013 Equity Incentive Plan. In addition, the Company awarded the Officer a bonus of 5,000 shares&#13;of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock at December 31, 2014 which vested immediately and were purchased by the Officer at par value.&#13;These shares were issued on January 9, 2015.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;Total compensation for these shares recorded at December 31, 2014 was $49,500&#13;based on the traded price of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock on that date.&amp;#160; There were no bonuses awarded the officer in&#13;2015.&amp;#160; Costs incurred pursuant to the Officer&amp;#146;s employment agreements for years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014 was&#13;$147,500 and $137,134, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Lease&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;On January 1, 2013, the Company entered into a five year and one&#13;month lease for space in Great Neck, New York, effective February 17, 2013, with base rent at $39,260, per year, subject to certain&#13;increases as defined.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;The lease agreement requires two months annual rent as a security deposit and the personal guaranty&#13;of the President of the Company. The rent is due in monthly installments commencing April 1, 2013; rent expense is being recorded&#13;on a straight line basis over the term of the lease.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;The difference between the rent payments made and straight line&#13;basis has been recorded as deferred rent. Rent expense, net of sublease&amp;#160;for the years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014 was&#13;$22,408 and $26,518, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Investor Relations Consulting Agreement&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;In August 2013, the Company entered into an Investor Relations&#13;Consulting Agreement (Agreement) with an investor relations firm to provide consulting services regarding financial markets and&#13;exchanges, competitors, business acquisitions and other aspects of or concerning the Company&amp;#146;s business. The Agreement is&#13;for a term of twelve months commencing August 16, 2013, with a one month cancellation option for either party. The Agreement called&#13;for a monthly consulting and services fee of $2,000. In addition, the Company agreed to grant to the consultant an aggregate of&#13;3,500 shares of the Company&amp;#146;s restricted stock, valued at $70,000, ($20.00, per share), the price of the stock, reflective&#13;of the post-split calculation, at the time of the Agreement. $52,500 of the consulting fee was recognized in 2013, with the remaining&#13;$17,500 recognized in 2014.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;On September 1, 2014, the Agreement was renewed and amended for&#13;a term of twelve months with the monthly service fee reduced to $1,500. During the years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014, $9,000&#13;and $18,500 in fees was incurred under this agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Merchandising Agreement&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;On May 5, 2014, the Company entered into&#13;an agreement to participate in a merchandising relationship which can be terminated by either party with forty-five days&#13;written notification to the other party.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;In consideration of its participation, the Company agreed to pay a&#13;monthly fee to the merchandiser of 4.0% of gross sales of the Company&amp;#146;s product.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;In accordance with the&#13;agreement, all slotting fees are waived on all new items and the merchandiser will review all new items brought into the&#13;warehouse six months from the initial distribution date to determine whether the item is selling at an appropriate rate. The&#13;Company will provide the merchandising group with competitive promotional allowances as defined. During the years ended&#13;December 31, 2015 $11,989 and $1,500 in fees was incurred under this agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Sales Representative Contract&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;Effective June 30, 2014, the Company entered into a contract with&#13;a sales representative to increase the demand for and promote the products of the Company and to provide marketing services as&#13;defined. In exchange for these services, the sales representative is entitled to a commission of 3.0% of net sales, as defined.&#13;There is no minimum monthly commission for the initial twelve months and the representative will also be entitled to an additional&#13;performance bonus, as defined. The contract is on a month to month basis and may be terminated by either party with thirty days&#13;written notice to the other party. As of December 31, 2015 and 2014, no fees were incurred under this agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Director Compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;In connection with the increase in the number of directors on the&#13;Board to four and the appointment of a new director to fill the vacancy on June 25, 2014, the Company agreed to grant 2,100 shares&#13;of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock to the new director which would vest in three equal installments, as defined. On December 4,&#13;2014, the director resigned from his position on the Board and agreed to accept 1,000, shares of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock&#13;as full compensation for his service to the Board valued at $10,000.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Social Media Agreement&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In August 2014, the Company entered into an&#13;agreement with a contractor to provide social media management services. The agreement continues through completion of the project&#13;and is subject to early cancellation with fifteen days&amp;#146; notice prior to the date of cancellation. Fees for the services are&#13;$3,179, per month. For the years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014, the Company incurred expense of $45,600 and $8,019 under the&#13;agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Food Broker Agreement&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In September 2014, the Company entered into&#13;an agreement appointing a food broker as its sole and exclusive representative for one year terms to provide services related to&#13;negotiating the sale of the Company&amp;#146;s products within a defined territory. The food broker will receive a guaranteed monthly&#13;income of $3,500 for the first seven months of the agreement and a commission of 5% on each sale to be computed on the net invoice&#13;price as defined. Until such time as the commissions reach $3,500 per month, the Company will continue to pay the $3,500 monthly&#13;income. The agreement will be in effect from year to year and may be terminated by either party with ninety days written notice.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;All&#13;commissions earned will be paid during the ninety day transition period and will continue for an additional ninety days after the&#13;termination date.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;For the years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014, the Company incurred expense of $31,500 and $10,500&#13;under the agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Public Relations Agreement&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Effective September 1, 2014, the Company entered&#13;into an agreement with a consultant to provide public relations services for a monthly retainer of $4,000 and 240 shares of the&#13;Company&amp;#146;s common stock to be issued equally in installments that vest over a twelve month period. The agreement may be terminated&#13;in writing with two months&amp;#146; notice.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;As of December 31, 2015 and 2014, the Company incurred expense of $32,000&#13;and $16,000 and issued 160 shares and 80 shares, of the Company&amp;#146;s common stock under the agreement recorded at a price of&#13;$10.00 per share.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Common Stock to be Issued&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;Management has estimated that an additional 1,361,434 shares of&#13;common stock (see Note 8) are required to be issued under various ratchet provisions.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;However, the actual amount of&#13;shares to be issued could be greater than the amount estimated by management.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;Litigation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;On May 2, 2014, an action was commenced against the Company and&#13;two of its officers in the Supreme Court of the State of New York, County of Nassau.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;The action relates to restricted&#13;shares of the Company acquired by the plaintiff which the plaintiff allegedly sought to sell.&amp;#160;&amp;#160;The complaint asserts&#13;claims under various theories, including conversion, breach of contract, breach of fiduciary duty, fraudulent misrepresentation&#13;and unjust enrichment, and seeks damages in excess of five million dollars.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
